3/31/17, 4:45â€¯PM - ğ”–ğ”ğ”¤ğ”ğ”¯: Whenever you go to bay area, try eating at one of these places -
3/31/17, 4:46â€¯PM - Pritam Bhattacharya: Ok
3/31/17, 4:47â€¯PM - ğ”–ğ”ğ”¤ğ”ğ”¯: 1. Anjappar Chettinad (in milpitas) - my fav restaurant! 
Eat: Chicken chettinad with naan, or Karaikudi chicken. Or for veg, Poondu Kuzhambu which is made of garlics. And take buttermilk!
2. Dee Dees (cupertino):
Go on a saturday for regional buffets - maharashtrian, gujarathi, rajasthani etc. Pani puri pan aste tithe.
3. Bawarchi (santa clara):
Ulavacharu biryani, and Vijaywada biryani is amazing.
4. TastySubs (santa clara):
Awesome Indian Pizzas. And they are named like "3 Idiots", "Gabbar Singh" etc haha
5. Red Hot Chilli Peppers (san mateo):
Indo-chinese food just like we get in india. Schezwan Rice, Schezwan noodles, chicken lollipop etc.
6. InChin's bamboo garden (santa clara)
Same as RHCP
7. Lotus (fremont):
Vijaywada biryani.
8. Peacock (santa clara)
Chicken masakhali
9. Banana Leaf (milpitas):
Really good malaysian food. The appetizers (Roti Paratha) is very good, like indian curry. And then main course dishes are also good, i dont remember the names
10. Saravana Bhavan  (fremont)
Really good south indian food (veg only). Dosa, uttappam, south indian thali, idli etc.
11. Tirupathi Bhimas (milpitas)
Really good south indian good just like saravana bhavan, but cheaper! 8$ madhe hota.
12. Le Soleil (in san leandro):
Amazing thai red curry chicken here.
